  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=6.4)
    While the cosmic setting is imaginative, the emotional arc follows a somewhat predictable redemption pattern. Phrases like "weathered heart" appear multiple times without variation. The writing occasionally tips into purple prose with phrases like "his voice carrying the weight of eons and the lightness of newfound hope." Some emotional transitions feel compressed rather than earned through nuanced development. However, the creative interpretation of the design studio and memory concepts demonstrates originality within the assigned elements.
